The opponent needs to bring all his pieces in the home region in order to take them out and so do you.\r\n\r\n‚úì You can move around the board in one direction. You move from the bottom-right corner to the bottom-left corner then to the top-left corner and finally to the top-right corner on a path that resembles a horseshoe.
